+					var $selecter = $("#selecter");
+					if($selecter.hasClass("open")) {
+						$selecter.removeClass("open");
+					} else {
+						$selecter.addClass("open");
+					}
+				})
+				$("#control-wrapper").on("click", ".title", function() {
+					var $list = $(this).siblings(),
+						$section = $list.parent();
+					if($section.hasClass("active")) {
+						$section.removeClass("active");
+					} else {
+						$(".section.active").removeClass("active")
+						$section.addClass("active");
+					}
+				});
+				//PC底部弹出二维码事件
+				$(".iconimg").hover(function() {
+					$(this).parent().addClass("active");
+				}, function() {

+				});

+		imageSize: new BMap.Size(32, 40)
+	});
+	var icon_red = new BMap.Icon("img/map/tb_xz.png", new BMap.Size(32, 40), {
+		imageSize: new BMap.Size(32, 40)
+	});
+	var opts = {
+		width: 280, // 信息窗口宽度
+		height: 0, // 信息窗口高度
+		title: "", // 信息窗口标题
+		enableMessage: true //设置允许信息窗发送短息
+	};
+	var markers = [];
+	for(var i = 0; i < data_info.length; i++) {
+		var marker = new BMap.Marker(new BMap.Point(data_info[i][0], data_info[i][1])); // 创建标注
+		var content = data_info[i][2];
+		marker.setIcon(icon);
+		markers.push(marker);
+		map.addOverlay(marker); // 将标注添加到地图中
+		addClickHandler(content, marker);
+	}
+
+	//跳转指定驾校
+	$("#control-wrapper").on("click", ".item", function() {
+		var id = $(this).attr("data-id"),
+			school = data_info[id],
+			marker = markers[id],
+			content = school[2],
+			point = new BMap.Point(school[0], school[1]);
+		$("#control-wrapper .selected").removeClass("selected");
+		$(this).addClass("selected");
+		map.setZoom(14);
+		map.panTo(point); //移动到指定坐标
+		getFocus(marker);
+		var infoWindow = new BMap.InfoWindow(content, opts); // 创建信息窗口对象 
+		map.openInfoWindow(infoWindow, point); //开启信息窗口
+	});
+	//移动端选择区域
+	$("#selecter").on("click",".item",function(){
+		var qu=$(this).attr("data-area");
+		goArea(qu,13);
+		$("#selecter").removeClass("open").find(".name").text(qu);
+	})
+	//PC端选择区域
+	$("#control-wrapper").on("click", ".title", function() {
+		var qu=$(this).attr("data-area");
+		goArea(qu,14);
+	})
+	
+	function addClickHandler(content, marker) {
+		marker.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
+			getFocus(marker)
+			openInfo(content, e)
+		});
+	}
+	//控制器,标注获取焦点
+	function getFocus(marker) {
+		var id = 0; //控制器item的data-id
+		for(var i = 0; i < markers.length; i++) {
+			markers[i].setIcon(icon);
+			if(markers[i] == marker) {
+				id = i;
+			}
+		}
+		marker.setIcon(icon_red);
+		$("#control-wrapper .item").each(function(i, n) {
+			var dataId = $(n).attr("data-id");
+			if(dataId == id) {
+				$("#control-wrapper .selected").removeClass("selected");
+				$("#control-wrapper .active").removeClass("active");
+				$(n).addClass("selected").parent().parent().addClass("active");
+			}
+		})
+	}
+
+	function openInfo(content, e) {
+		var p = e.target;
+		var point = new BMap.Point(p.getPosition().lng, p.getPosition().lat);
+		var infoWindow = new BMap.InfoWindow(content, opts); // 创建信息窗口对象 
+		map.openInfoWindow(infoWindow, point); //开启信息窗口
+	}
+	var local = new BMap.LocalSearch(map, {
+		renderOptions: {
+			map: map
+		}
+	});
+
+	function goQu(qu) {
+		local.search(qu);
+		setTimeout(function() {
+			console.log(qu + ":" + map.getCenter().lng + "," + map.getCenter().lat);
+		}, 2000);
+	}
+
+	function goArea(qu,zoom) {
+		var point = data_area[qu];
+		var zoom=zoom||14;
+		map.setZoom(zoom);
+		map.panTo(new BMap.Point(point[0], point[1]));
+	}
+
+	//获取URL中参数
+	function getUrlParam(name) {
+		//构造一个含有目标参数的正则表达式对象
+		var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)" + name + "=([^&]*)(&|$)");
+		//匹配目标参数
+		var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg);
+		//返回参数值
+		if(r != null) return decodeURI(r[2]);
+		return null;
+	}
+</script>
